踪影

While having fewer eyes in the store increased profits for chains in those decades, it has left stores in court cases without as many visible personnel to deter shoplifting, crime prevention experts say.;犯罪预防专家说，虽然在过去几十年中，人们对商店的关注减少了，连锁店的利润增加了，但在法庭上，商店里却没有那么多可见的人员来阻止商店盗窃。
